================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);

end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_18_Charger_Speed/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP '18 Charger Speed → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Explorer/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Explorer → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)

    Parent: TDPatterns

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Highway_Patrol/BCHP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Highway Patrol → BCHP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:38
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;
